### [189] [Mixed-Precision Performance Portability of FFT-Based GPU-Accelerated Algorithms for Block-Triangular Toeplitz Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10202)
*Sreeram Venkat,Kasia Swirydowicz,Noah Wolfe,Omar Ghattas*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种性能可移植性框架，使 FFTMatvec 应用能在 AMD GPU 上高效运行，并结合混合精度和帕累托优化，在多种 AMD GPU 上取得了优异性能，并成功扩展至大规模计算环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着领导级计算设施硬件多样性的增加以及 GPU 在低精度计算中展现出的巨大性能提升，科学 HPC 工作流采用混合精度算法和性能可移植性模型具有强大的驱动力。

Method: 该研究提出了一种使用 Hipify 的即时框架来实现性能可移植性，并将其应用于计算块三角 Toeplitz 矩阵的矩阵向量乘法（FFTMatvec）应用。该方法能够使原本仅支持 CUDA 的 FFTMatvec 应用在 AMD GPU 上实现优异的性能。此外，该研究还集成了一个动态混合精度框架，并利用帕累托前沿分析来确定满足特定误差容忍度的最佳混合精度配置。

Result: FFTMatvec 应用已成功实现性能可移植性，可在 AMD GPU 上运行。通过集成到 rocBLAS 库中，无需更改应用代码即可实现性能优化。研究提出了动态混合精度框架，并通过帕累托前沿分析确定了最佳混合精度配置，该配置在 AMD Instinct MI250X、MI300X 和 MI355X GPU 上表现优异。此外，该性能可移植、混合精度的 FFTMatvec 已成功扩展至 OLCF Frontier 超级计算机上的 2,048 个 GPU。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了一种使用 Hipify 框架实现性能可移植性的方法，并将其应用于 FFTMatvec 应用，使其能够在 AMD GPU 上无缝运行并获得优异性能。通过将性能优化集成到 rocBLAS 库中，并采用动态混合精度框架和帕累托前沿分析，确定了在给定误差容忍度下的最优混合精度配置。该方法已在 AMD Instinct MI250X、MI300X 和 MI355X GPU 上进行了验证，并在 OLCF Frontier 超级计算机上扩展到 2,048 个 GPU。

Abstract: The hardware diversity displayed in leadership-class computing facilities,
alongside the immense performance boosts exhibited by today's GPUs when
computing in lower precision, provide a strong incentive for scientific HPC
workflows to adopt mixed-precision algorithms and performance portability
models. We present an on-the-fly framework using Hipify for performance
portability and apply it to FFTMatvec-an HPC application that computes
matrix-vector products with block-triangular Toeplitz matrices. Our approach
enables FFTMatvec, initially a CUDA-only application, to run seamlessly on AMD
GPUs with excellent observed performance. Performance optimizations for AMD
GPUs are integrated directly into the open-source rocBLAS library, keeping the
application code unchanged. We then present a dynamic mixed-precision framework
for FFTMatvec; a Pareto front analysis determines the optimal mixed-precision
configuration for a desired error tolerance. Results are shown for AMD Instinct
MI250X, MI300X, and the newly launched MI355X GPUs. The performance-portable,
mixed-precision FFTMatvec is scaled to 2,048 GPUs on the OLCF Frontier
supercomputer.

</details>


### [190] [Hard Shell, Reliable Core: Improving Resilience in Replicated Systems with Selective Hybridization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10141)
*Laura Lawniczak,Tobias Distler*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: ShellFT是一个允许根据特定用例需求灵活选择拜占庭容错复制逻辑部分的框架，并通过微复制技术显著降低了分化成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的混合方法在容错和拜占庭容错的系统部分组合方面灵活性有限，并且存在显著的分化开销。

Method: 利用微复制的概念，允许系统设计者自由选择复制逻辑中需要拜占庭容错的部分，并通过三种自定义ShellFT协议和分析其实现复杂性来说明其灵活性。

Result: 与传统的混合方法相比，ShellFT能够将分化成本降低70%以上。

Conclusion: ShellFT框架通过微复制概念实现了选择性混合，允许系统设计者自由选择需要拜占庭容错的复制逻辑部分，从而为个别用例的特定特性和需求量身定制混合解决方案，与传统的混合方法相比，可以将分化成本降低70%以上。

Abstract: Hybrid fault models are known to be an effective means for enhancing the
robustness of consensus-based replicated systems. However, existing
hybridization approaches suffer from limited flexibility with regard to the
composition of crash-tolerant and Byzantine fault-tolerant system parts and/or
are associated with a significant diversification overhead. In this paper we
address these issues with ShellFT, a framework that leverages the concept of
micro replication to allow system designers to freely choose the parts of the
replication logic that need to be resilient against Byzantine faults. As a key
benefit, such a selective hybridization makes it possible to develop hybrid
solutions that are tailored to the specific characteristics and requirements of
individual use cases. To illustrate this flexibility, we present three custom
ShellFT protocols and analyze the complexity of their implementations. Our
evaluation shows that compared with traditional hybridization approaches,
ShellFT is able to decrease diversification costs by more than 70%.

</details>


### [191] [GPZ: GPU-Accelerated Lossy Compressor for Particle Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10305)
*Ruoyu Li,Yafan Huang,Longtao Zhang,Zhuoxun Yang,Sheng Di,Jiajun Huang,Jinyang Liu,Jiannan Tian,Xin Liang,Guanpeng Li,Hanqi Guo,Franck Cappello,Kai Zhao*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子模拟和点云应用产生海量、不规则的数据集，对存储、I/O 和实时分析提出了挑战，而传统压缩技术难以应对。

Method: GPZ 采用新颖的四阶段并行流水线，并针对计算、内存访问和 GPU 占用率进行了优化。

Result: GPZ 的吞吐量是五个最先进的 GPU 压缩器的 8 倍，同时实现了更高的压缩率和数据质量。

Conclusion: GPZ 在三种不同的 GPU 架构上使用六个大规模、真实的科学数据集进行了广泛的评估，在压缩效率、吞吐量和数据质量方面均优于其他压缩器。

Abstract: Particle-based simulations and point-cloud applications generate massive,
irregular datasets that challenge storage, I/O, and real-time analytics.
Traditional compression techniques struggle with irregular particle
distributions and GPU architectural constraints, often resulting in limited
throughput and suboptimal compression ratios. In this paper, we present GPZ, a
high-performance, error-bounded lossy compressor designed specifically for
large-scale particle data on modern GPUs. GPZ employs a novel four-stage
parallel pipeline that synergistically balances high compression efficiency
with the architectural demands of massively parallel hardware. We introduce a
suite of targeted optimizations for computation, memory access, and GPU
occupancy that enables GPZ to achieve near-hardware-limit throughput. We
conduct an extensive evaluation on three distinct GPU architectures
(workstation, data center, and edge) using six large-scale, real-world
scientific datasets from five distinct domains. The results demonstrate that
GPZ consistently and significantly outperforms five state-of-the-art GPU
compressors, delivering up to 8x higher end-to-end throughput while
simultaneously achieving superior compression ratios and data quality.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Fine-tuning foundation models is critical for superior performance on

but limited client data and heterogeneous data distributions hinder effective
collaboration. To address the challenge, we propose a flexible personalized
federated learning paradigm that enables clients to engage in collaborative
learning while maintaining personalized objectives. Given the limited and
heterogeneous computational resources available on clients, we introduce
\textbf{flexible personalized split federated learning (FlexP-SFL)}. Based on
split learning, FlexP-SFL allows each client to train a portion of the model
locally while offloading the rest to a server, according to resource
constraints. Additionally, we propose an alignment strategy to improve
personalized model performance on global data. Experimental results show that
FlexP-SFL outperforms baseline models in personalized fine-tuning efficiency
and final accuracy.

### [194] [Introducing CQ: A C-like API for Quantum Accelerated HPC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10854)
*Oliver Thomson Brown,Mateusz Meller,James Richings*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: CQ is a new API and simulator (CQ-SimBE) for integrating quantum computing into HPC codes, offering C-like functionality and fine-grained control.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To enable the incremental integration of quantum computing into classical HPC codes by providing a C-like API and a reference implementation.

Method: CQ is a specification for a C-like API for quantum accelerated HPC, and CQ-SimBE is a reference implementation of CQ written in C99, built on top of the statevector simulator QuEST. CQ supports runtime offloading from languages such as C and Fortran, is compatible with strictly and strongly typed compiled languages, and gives the programmer fine-grained control over classical data movement.

Result: CQ enables the incremental integration of quantum computing into classical HPC codes by supporting runtime offloading and fine-grained control over classical data movement. CQ-SimBE demonstrates the utility of CQ and allows experimentation with new features.

Conclusion: CQ and CQ-SimBE are open-source and available in public repositories, enabling incremental integration of quantum computing into classical HPC codes.

Abstract: In this paper we present CQ, a specification for a C-like API for quantum
accelerated HPC, as well as CQ-SimBE, a reference implementation of CQ written
in C99, and built on top of the statevector simulator QuEST. CQ focuses on
enabling the incremental integration of quantum computing into classical HPC
codes by supporting runtime offloading from languages such as C and Fortran. It
provides a way of describing and offloading quantum computations which is
compatible with strictly and strongly typed compiled languages, and gives the
programmer fine-grained control over classical data movement. The CQ Simulated
Backend (CQ-SimBE) provides both a way to demonstrate the usage and utility of
CQ, and a space to experiment with new features such as support for analogue
quantum computing. Both the CQ specification and CQ-SimBE are open-source, and
available in public repositories.

</details>

Abstract: Minimmit is a new protocol for State-Machine-Replication (SMR) that extends

### [196] [B-repLer: Semantic B-rep Latent Editor using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10201)
*Yilin Liu,Niladri Shekhar Dutt,Changjian Li,Niloy J. Mitra*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: B-repLer是一种针对B-rep CAD对象进行文本驱动编辑的微调mLLM，解决了现有mLLM在3D任务中的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决mLLMs在3D分析和编辑任务中的局限性，特别是处理工程对象行业标准但脆弱的B-rep表示的挑战。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的多模态架构，专门用于处理B-rep模型，并利用现有的CAD工具与mLLMs结合，自动生成所需的推理数据集，无需外部注释。

Result: B-repLer能够理解文本提示并对B-rep进行语义编辑，生成有效输出，并在各种复杂性的文本驱动B-rep编辑方面取得了成功。

Conclusion: B-repLer可以理解文本提示并在给定的B-rep上进行语义编辑以生成有效输出，实现了之前无法实现的文本驱动的B-rep编辑。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (mLLMs), trained in a mixed modal setting as
a universal model, have been shown to compete with or even outperform many
specialized algorithms for imaging and graphics tasks. As demonstrated across
many applications, mLLMs' ability to jointly process image and text data makes
them suitable for zero-shot applications or efficient fine-tuning towards
specialized tasks. However, they have had limited success in 3D analysis and
editing tasks. This is due to both the lack of suitable (annotated) 3D data as
well as the idiosyncrasies of 3D representations. In this paper, we investigate
whether mLLMs can be adapted to support high-level editing of Boundary
Representation (B-rep) CAD objects. B-reps remain the industry-standard for
precisely encoding engineering objects, but are challenging as the
representation is fragile (i.e. can easily lead to invalid CAD objects) and no
publicly available data source exists with semantically-annotated B-reps or CAD
construction history. We present B-repLer as a finetuned mLLM that can
understand text prompts and make semantic edits on given B-Reps to produce
valid outputs. We enable this via a novel multimodal architecture, specifically
designed to handle B-rep models, and demonstrate how existing CAD tools, in
conjunction with mLLMs, can be used to automatically generate the required
reasoning dataset, without relying on external annotations. We extensively
evaluate B-repLer and demonstrate several text-based B-rep edits of various
complexity, which were not previously possible.

</details>

*Sayan Nag,K J Joseph,Koustava Goswami,Vlad I Morariu,Balaji Vasan Srinivasan*

Motivation: 评估图形设计需要从对齐、构图、美学和颜色选择等多个方面进行考量。为了实现对设计的整体评估，需要整合多位专家评审员的反馈。因此，有必要开发一种能够有效进行设计评估的系统。

Result: 通过与针对问题设置调整过的现有基线方法进行详尽的实验评估，并辅以关键的消融实验，证明了 Agentic-DRS 在评估图形设计和生成可操作反馈方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为 AgenticDRS 的代理设计评审系统，该系统通过多个代理协同分析设计，并由一个元代理进行协调，在评估图形设计方面表现出有效性，并能生成可操作的反馈。作者希望这项工作能引起对这一实用但未充分探索的研究方向的关注。

Abstract: Evaluating graphic designs involves assessing it from multiple facets like
alignment, composition, aesthetics and color choices. Evaluating designs in a
holistic way involves aggregating feedback from individual expert reviewers.
Towards this, we propose an Agentic Design Review System (AgenticDRS), where
multiple agents collaboratively analyze a design, orchestrated by a meta-agent.
A novel in-context exemplar selection approach based on graph matching and a
unique prompt expansion method plays central role towards making each agent
design aware. Towards evaluating this framework, we propose DRS-BENCH
benchmark. Thorough experimental evaluation against state-of-the-art baselines
adapted to the problem setup, backed-up with critical ablation experiments
brings out the efficacy of Agentic-DRS in evaluating graphic designs and
generating actionable feedback. We hope that this work will attract attention
to this pragmatic, yet under-explored research direction.

"reasoning ability" of LLMs are just illusions of those people who with vague
concepts. In fact, the LLMs can never have the true understanding ability and
true reasoning ability. This paper intents to explain that, because the
essential limitations of their working principle, the LLMs can never have the
ability of true correct reasoning.

*Alexandru-Andrei Avram,Adrian Groza,Alexandru Lecu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究提出了一种包含四个智能体（机器学习、维基百科知识检查、一致性检测、网页抓取数据分析）的多智能体系统，利用关系抽取来检测新闻标题和短文本中的虚假信息。该系统通过MCP协调，达到了95.3%的准确率和0.964的F1分数，优于单一智能体和传统方法，且易于扩展。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于关系抽取的多智能体系统，用于检测新闻标题和短文本片段中的虚假信息。该系统包含四个智能体：(i) 逻辑回归机器学习智能体，(ii) 依赖命名实体识别的维基百科知识检查智能体，(iii) 利用大型语言模型提示工程的一致性检测智能体，(iv) 用于提取关系三元组以进行事实核查的网络抓取数据分析智能体。系统通过模型上下文协议（MCP）进行协调，实现了组件间的共享上下文和实时学习。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的多智能体系统通过结合机器学习、维基百科知识检查、一致性检测和网页抓取数据分析，在新闻标题和短文本片段的虚假信息检测方面表现出色，准确率达到95.3%，F1得分为0.964，显著优于单一智能体和传统方法。研究还表明，基于误分类率加权聚合的方法优于阈值优化，并且该系统的模块化设计易于扩展且能保留决策过程的细节。

Abstract: The large spread of disinformation across digital platforms creates
significant challenges to information integrity. This paper presents a
multi-agent system that uses relation extraction to detect disinformation in
news articles, focusing on titles and short text snippets. The proposed Agentic
AI system combines four agents: (i) a machine learning agent (logistic
regression), (ii) a Wikipedia knowledge check agent (which relies on named
entity recognition), (iii) a coherence detection agent (using LLM prompt
engineering), and (iv) a web-scraped data analyzer that extracts relational
triplets for fact checking. The system is orchestrated via the Model Context
Protocol (MCP), offering shared context and live learning across components.
Results demonstrate that the multi-agent ensemble achieves 95.3% accuracy with
an F1 score of 0.964, significantly outperforming individual agents and
traditional approaches. The weighted aggregation method, mathematically derived
from individual agent misclassification rates, proves superior to algorithmic
threshold optimization. The modular architecture makes the system easily
scalable, while also maintaining details of the decision processes.

Abstract: We focus here on Deep Research Agents (DRAs), which are systems that can take

utilize, internet-based content to address the prompt. Recent DRAs have

research largely involves proprietary closed-source systems. At the time of

In this work we adapt the challenging recent BrowseComp benchmark to compare

introduce three strategic improvements to ODR, resulting in the ODR+ model,

*Bin Hong,Jiayu Liu,Zhenya Huang,Kai Zhang,Mengdi Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型推理模型（LRMs）太长了，而且很慢。我们提出了 LCPO，一种新的优化方法，可以将输出长度减半，同时保持性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型（LRMs）在复杂任务中表现出色，但其冗长的输出带来了高昂的计算成本和过度思考的风险，如何在保证推理效果的同时提高效率是一个关键挑战。

Method: 本研究通过分析生成路径分布和难度估计来过滤生成轨迹，并考察了 Bradley-Terry 损失框架下各种偏好优化方法的收敛行为，在此基础上提出了 LCPO，直接平衡了与 NLL 损失相关的隐式奖励，实现了对生成长度的有效控制。

Result: 实验证明，LCPO 能够显著减少 50% 以上的平均输出长度，同时保持推理性能，证明了该方法在引导 LRM 实现高效推理方面的潜力。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) have demonstrated strong
performance on complex tasks through long Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning.
However, their lengthy outputs increase computational costs and may lead to
overthinking, raising challenges in balancing reasoning effectiveness and
efficiency. Current methods for efficient reasoning often compromise reasoning
quality or require extensive resources. This paper investigates efficient
methods to reduce the generation length of LRMs. We analyze generation path
distributions and filter generated trajectories through difficulty estimation.
Subsequently, we analyze the convergence behaviors of the objectives of various
preference optimization methods under a Bradley-Terry loss based framework.
Based on the analysis, we propose Length Controlled Preference Optimization
(LCPO) that directly balances the implicit reward related to NLL loss. LCPO can
effectively learn length preference with limited data and training. Extensive
experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly reduces the average
output length by over 50\% across multiple benchmarks while maintaining the
reasoning performance. Our work highlights the potential for computationally
efficient approaches in guiding LRMs toward efficient reasoning.

### [205] [KompeteAI: Accelerated Autonomous Multi-Agent System for End-to-End Pipeline Generation for Machine Learning Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10177)
*Stepan Kulibaba,Artem Dzhalilov,Roman Pakhomov,Oleg Svidchenko,Alexander Gasnikov,Aleksei Shpilman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: KompeteAI是一个新颖的AutoML框架，通过动态探索、合并优秀方案、整合RAG和预测评分模型，解决了现有AutoML系统的局限性，并在基准测试中取得了领先成果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的LLM驱动的AutoML系统虽然能力出众，但面临着探索策略受限和执行瓶颈等严峻挑战。具体而言，探索受限于缺乏多样性的一次性方法和无法重组强部分解的MCTS方法；执行瓶颈则源于冗长的代码验证周期，阻碍了迭代优化。

Method: KompeteAI框架采用动态解决方案空间探索，引入了包括合并优秀候选方案在内的第一阶段，并结合检索增强生成（RAG）技术，从Kaggle notebooks和arXiv论文中汲取真实世界策略，以扩展假设空间。此外，KompeteAI通过预测评分模型和加速调试方法解决了执行瓶颈，利用早期指标评估解决方案潜力，避免了昂贵的完全代码执行，并将评估速度提高了6.9倍。

Result: KompeteAI通过其创新的方法，在AutoML基准测试MLE-Bench上，平均性能超越了RD-agent、AIDE和Ml-Master等领先方法3%。同时，提出的Kompete-bench基准也解决了MLE-Bench的局限性，KompeteAI在该新基准上也达到了最先进水平。

Conclusion: KompeteAI在MLE-Bench和Kompete-bench基准测试上均取得了最先进的成果，平均比现有领先方法（如RD-agent, AIDE, Ml-Master）高出3%。

Abstract: Recent Large Language Model (LLM)-based AutoML systems demonstrate impressive
capabilities but face significant limitations such as constrained exploration
strategies and a severe execution bottleneck. Exploration is hindered by
one-shot methods lacking diversity and Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)
approaches that fail to recombine strong partial solutions. The execution
bottleneck arises from lengthy code validation cycles that stifle iterative
refinement. To overcome these challenges, we introduce KompeteAI, a novel
AutoML framework with dynamic solution space exploration. Unlike previous MCTS
methods that treat ideas in isolation, KompeteAI introduces a merging stage
that composes top candidates. We further expand the hypothesis space by
integrating Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG), sourcing ideas from Kaggle
notebooks and arXiv papers to incorporate real-world strategies. KompeteAI also
addresses the execution bottleneck via a predictive scoring model and an
accelerated debugging method, assessing solution potential using early stage
metrics to avoid costly full-code execution. This approach accelerates pipeline
evaluation 6.9 times. KompeteAI outperforms leading methods (e.g., RD-agent,
AIDE, and Ml-Master) by an average of 3\% on the primary AutoML benchmark,

entropy of a system -- can enhance uncertainty quantification, decision-making,

formulation in physics, the framework is adapted for AI by introducing an
event-centric measure that captures how actions, observations, or other
discrete occurrences impact uncertainty at future time horizons. Both the
original and AI-adjusted definitions of entropic potential are formalized, with

potential to unify and strengthen uncertainty modeling in intelligent systems.

framework offers a theoretically grounded, interpretable, and versatile
approach to managing uncertainty in AI, bridging principles from

### [207] [Promoting Efficient Reasoning with Verifiable Stepwise Reward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10293)

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型（LRM）通常会过度思考，在简单问题上花费过多的计算量，从而降低了效率。现有的高效推理方法通常需要准确的任务评估来预设令牌预算或选择推理模式，这限制了它们的灵活性和可靠性。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的基于规则的可验证分步奖励机制（VSRM），该机制根据推理轨迹中中间状态的表现来分配奖励。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在实现大幅缩减输出长度的同时，保持了原有的推理性能，在效率和准确性之间取得了最佳平衡。

Conclusion: 该方法有效抑制了无效步骤并鼓励了有效推理，从根本上缓解了过度思考问题。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) have recently achieved significant progress in
complex reasoning tasks, aided by reinforcement learning with verifiable
rewards. However, LRMs often suffer from overthinking, expending excessive
computation on simple problems and reducing efficiency. Existing efficient
reasoning methods typically require accurate task assessment to preset token
budgets or select reasoning modes, which limits their flexibility and
reliability. In this work, we revisit the essence of overthinking and identify
that encouraging effective steps while penalizing ineffective ones is key to
its solution. To this end, we propose a novel rule-based verifiable stepwise
reward mechanism (VSRM), which assigns rewards based on the performance of
intermediate states in the reasoning trajectory. This approach is intuitive and
naturally fits the step-by-step nature of reasoning tasks. We conduct extensive
experiments on standard mathematical reasoning benchmarks, including AIME24 and
AIME25, by integrating VSRM with PPO and Reinforce++. Results show that our
method achieves substantial output length reduction while maintaining original
reasoning performance, striking an optimal balance between efficiency and
accuracy. Further analysis of overthinking frequency and pass@k score before
and after training demonstrates that our approach in deed effectively
suppresses ineffective steps and encourages effective reasoning, fundamentally
alleviating the overthinking problem. All code will be released upon
acceptance.

### [209] [Multi-Agent Trust Region Policy Optimisation: A Joint Constraint Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10340)
*Chak Lam Shek,Guangyao Shi,Pratap Tokekar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的HATRPO方法为每个智能体分配相同的KL阈值，这在异构设置中可能导致训练缓慢和局部最优更新。

Method: 提出两种分配KL散度阈值的方法：HATRPO-W（一种基于KKT的方法，用于在全局KL约束下优化阈值分配）和HATRPO-G（一种基于改进与散度比率优先考虑智能体的贪婪算法）。

Result: HATRPO-W和HATRPO-G在各种多智能体强化学习基准测试中，相比基线方法，都实现了更快的收敛速度和更高的最终奖励，性能提升超过22.5%。HATRPO-W的学习动态更稳定，方差更低。

Conclusion: 所提出的HATRPO-W和HATRPO-G方法在异构多智能体强化学习设置中显著提高了HATRPO的性能，实现了更快的收敛速度和更高的最终奖励，在最终性能上均超越了22.5%。HATRPO-W还表现出更稳定的学习动态，其方差较低。

Abstract: Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) requires coordinated and stable
policy updates among interacting agents. Heterogeneous-Agent Trust Region
Policy Optimization (HATRPO) enforces per-agent trust region constraints using
Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence to stabilize training. However, assigning each
agent the same KL threshold can lead to slow and locally optimal updates,
especially in heterogeneous settings. To address this limitation, we propose
two approaches for allocating the KL divergence threshold across agents:
HATRPO-W, a Karush-Kuhn-Tucker-based (KKT-based) method that optimizes
threshold assignment under global KL constraints, and HATRPO-G, a greedy
algorithm that prioritizes agents based on improvement-to-divergence ratio. By
connecting sequential policy optimization with constrained threshold
scheduling, our approach enables more flexible and effective learning in
heterogeneous-agent settings. Experimental results demonstrate that our methods
significantly boost the performance of HATRPO, achieving faster convergence and
higher final rewards across diverse MARL benchmarks. Specifically, HATRPO-W and
HATRPO-G achieve comparable improvements in final performance, each exceeding
22.5%. Notably, HATRPO-W also demonstrates more stable learning dynamics, as
reflected by its lower variance.

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) plays a crucial role in grounding Large
Language Models by leveraging external knowledge, whereas the effectiveness is
often compromised by the retrieval of contextually flawed or incomplete
information. To address this, knowledge graph-based RAG methods have evolved
towards hierarchical structures, organizing knowledge into multi-level
summaries. However, these approaches still suffer from two critical,
unaddressed challenges: high-level conceptual summaries exist as disconnected
``semantic islands'', lacking the explicit relations needed for cross-community
reasoning; and the retrieval process itself remains structurally unaware, often
degenerating into an inefficient flat search that fails to exploit the graph's
rich topology. To overcome these limitations, we introduce LeanRAG, a framework
that features a deeply collaborative design combining knowledge aggregation and
retrieval strategies. LeanRAG first employs a novel semantic aggregation
algorithm that forms entity clusters and constructs new explicit relations
among aggregation-level summaries, creating a fully navigable semantic network.
Then, a bottom-up, structure-guided retrieval strategy anchors queries to the
most relevant fine-grained entities and then systematically traverses the
graph's semantic pathways to gather concise yet contextually comprehensive
evidence sets. The LeanRAG can mitigate the substantial overhead associated
with path retrieval on graphs and minimizes redundant information retrieval.
Extensive experiments on four challenging QA benchmarks with different domains
demonstrate that LeanRAG significantly outperforming existing methods in
response quality while reducing 46\% retrieval redundancy. Code is available
at: https://github.com/RaZzzyz/LeanRAG

capabilities across various tasks, but still struggle with complex mathematical
reasoning. Existing research primarily focuses on dataset construction and
method optimization, often overlooking two critical aspects: comprehensive
knowledge-driven design and model-centric data space modeling. In this paper,
we introduce We-Math 2.0, a unified system that integrates a structured
mathematical knowledge system, model-centric data space modeling, and a
reinforcement learning (RL)-based training paradigm to comprehensively enhance
the mathematical reasoning abilities of MLLMs. The key contributions of We-Math
2.0 are fourfold: (1) MathBook Knowledge System: We construct a five-level
hierarchical system encompassing 491 knowledge points and 1,819 fundamental
principles. (2) MathBook-Standard & Pro: We develop MathBook-Standard, a
dataset that ensures broad conceptual coverage and flexibility through dual
expansion. Additionally, we define a three-dimensional difficulty space and
generate 7 progressive variants per problem to build MathBook-Pro, a
challenging dataset for robust training. (3) MathBook-RL: We propose a
two-stage RL framework comprising: (i) Cold-Start Fine-tuning, which aligns the
model with knowledge-oriented chain-of-thought reasoning; and (ii) Progressive
Alignment RL, leveraging average-reward learning and dynamic data scheduling to
achieve progressive alignment across difficulty levels. (4) MathBookEval: We
introduce a comprehensive benchmark covering all 491 knowledge points with
diverse reasoning step distributions. Experimental results show that
MathBook-RL performs competitively with existing baselines on four widely-used
benchmarks and achieves strong results on MathBookEval, suggesting promising
generalization in mathematical reasoning.

0.90 ROUGE-L for query accuracy and 0.85 RelaxedEM for result accuracy on the
test set.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PASS（概率代理超网采样）是一个多模态框架，通过自适应地对多工具图上的代理工作流进行采样，产生带有可解释概率的决策路径。它利用对代理超网的已学习任务条件分布，在每个超网层自适应地选择最合适的工具，为事后审计提供带概率的轨迹，并直接增强医疗人工智能安全。PASS 还将关键发现压缩到不断发展的个性化内存中，同时动态决定是深化推理路径还是为了效率而提前退出。为了优化平衡性能和成本的帕累托前沿，我们设计了一种新颖的三阶段训练程序，包括专家知识热身、对比路径排序和成本感知强化学习。我们引入了 CAB-E，一个用于多步、安全关键、自由格式 CXR 推理的综合基准。

Result: PASS 在准确性、AUC、LLM-J 等多个指标上显著优于强基线，同时平衡了计算成本。

Conclusion: PASS 在准确性、AUC、LLM-J 等多个指标上显著优于强基线，同时平衡了计算成本，推动了可解释、自适应和多模态医疗器械系统的新范式。

Abstract: Existing tool-augmented agentic systems are limited in the real world by (i)
black-box reasoning steps that undermine trust of decision-making and pose
safety risks, (ii) poor multimodal integration, which is inherently critical
for healthcare tasks, and (iii) rigid and computationally inefficient agentic
pipelines. We introduce PASS (Probabilistic Agentic Supernet Sampling), the
first multimodal framework to address these challenges in the context of Chest
X-Ray (CXR) reasoning. PASS adaptively samples agentic workflows over a
multi-tool graph, yielding decision paths annotated with interpretable
probabilities. Given the complex CXR reasoning task with multimodal medical
data, PASS leverages its learned task-conditioned distribution over the agentic
supernet. Thus, it adaptively selects the most suitable tool at each supernet
layer, offering probability-annotated trajectories for post-hoc audits and
directly enhancing medical AI safety. PASS also continuously compresses salient
findings into an evolving personalized memory, while dynamically deciding
whether to deepen its reasoning path or invoke an early exit for efficiency. To
optimize a Pareto frontier balancing performance and cost, we design a novel
three-stage training procedure, including expert knowledge warm-up, contrastive
path-ranking, and cost-aware reinforcement learning. To facilitate rigorous
evaluation, we introduce CAB-E, a comprehensive benchmark for multi-step,
safety-critical, free-form CXR reasoning. Experiments across various benchmarks
validate that PASS significantly outperforms strong baselines in multiple
metrics (e.g., accuracy, AUC, LLM-J.) while balancing computational costs,
pushing a new paradigm shift towards interpretable, adaptive, and multimodal
medical agentic systems.

### [219] [Diversity First, Quality Later: A Two-Stage Assumption for Language Model Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10530)
*Zetian Sun,Dongfang Li,Baotian Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了“对齐阶段假设”，区分了语言模型对齐中的偏好注入和偏好微调阶段，并提出了一种识别这两个阶段边界的算法，旨在优化语言模型与人类偏好的对齐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型（LM）与人类偏好对齐对于构建可靠的AI系统至关重要。虽然直接偏好优化（DPO）及其基于在线抽样的方法在对齐方面取得了进展，但在线抽样数据并非总是最优，并且在不同模型上表现出效果差异。本研究旨在探究这种现象的原因，并提出改进方法。

Method: 本研究提出了“对齐阶段假设”，将语言模型对齐过程分为偏好注入阶段和偏好微调阶段，并提出了一种算法来识别这两个阶段之间的边界。通过理论和实证分析来解释和验证该假设，并在多种模型和对齐方法上进行了实验。

Result: 研究表明，在线抽样数据并非总是最优，并提出了“对齐阶段假设”来解释静态和在线偏好数据效果差异的现象。该假设将对齐过程分为两个阶段：偏好注入阶段（受益于多样性数据）和偏好微调阶段（偏好高质量数据）。通过理论和实证分析，研究提出了一个有效算法来识别这两个阶段的边界，并在多种模型和对齐方法上验证了该假设和算法的有效性。

Conclusion: 现有的语言模型（LM）对齐方法，如直接偏好优化（DPO）及其改进版本，在利用静态或在线抽样偏好数据进行模型优化时，表现出效果差异。本研究提出了“对齐阶段假设”，将对齐过程分为两个阶段：偏好注入阶段（需要多样化数据）和偏好微调阶段（需要高质量数据）。通过理论和实证分析，我们明确了这些阶段的特征，并提出了一种有效算法来识别它们之间的边界。在5个模型（Llama、Zephyr、Phi-2、Qwen、Pythia）和2种对齐方法（DPO、SLiC-HF）上的实验证明了对齐阶段假设及其边界测量的普适性。

Abstract: The alignment of language models (LMs) with human preferences is critical for
building reliable AI systems. The problem is typically framed as optimizing an
LM policy to maximize the expected reward that reflects human preferences.
Recently, Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) was proposed as a LM alignment
method that directly optimize the policy from static preference data, and
further improved by incorporating on-policy sampling (i.e., preference
candidates generated during the training loop) for better LM alignment.
However, we show on-policy data is not always optimal, with systematic
effectiveness difference emerging between static and on-policy preference
candidates. For example, on-policy data can result in a 3$\times$ effectiveness
compared with static data for Llama-3, and a 0.4$\times$ effectiveness for
Zephyr. To explain the phenomenon, we propose the alignment stage assumption,
which divides the alignment process into two distinct stages: the preference
injection stage, which benefits from diverse data, and the preference
fine-tuning stage, which favors high-quality data. Through theoretical and
empirical analysis, we characterize these stages and propose an effective
algorithm to identify the boundaries between them. We perform experiments on 5
models (Llama, Zephyr, Phi-2, Qwen, Pythia) and 2 alignment methods (DPO,
SLiC-HF) to show the generalizability of alignment stage assumption and
boundary measurement.

### [220] [Improving Value-based Process Verifier via Low-Cost Variance Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10539)
*Zetian Sun,Dongfang Li,Baotian Hu,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为了解决LLM推理中的估计误差问题，本文提出了一种名为ComMCS的新方法，通过结合不同步骤的MC估计量来降低方差并保持无偏性，且不增加额外成本。实验结果证明了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在许多任务中表现出色，但在数学等复杂领域的推理能力仍面临挑战。值基过程验证器是提高推理能力的有效途径，但其训练标注中的估计误差（由LLM推理成本高昂导致的有限MC样本量引起）限制了其效果。

Method: 提出了一种名为ComMCS（Compound Monte Carlo Sampling）的新方法，该方法通过线性组合当前和后续步骤的MC估计量来构建一个无偏估计量，以解决值基过程验证器中因蒙特卡洛（MC）样本量有限导致的估计误差问题。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为ComMCS（Compound Monte Carlo Sampling）的新方法，通过线性组合当前和后续步骤的MC估计量来构建一个无偏估计量，从而解决了值基过程验证器在LLM推理中估计误差的问题。理论上证明了该方法能在不增加额外LLM推理成本的情况下，可预测地降低方差并保持估计的无偏性。实验证明ComMCS在MATH-500和GSM8K基准测试中优于其他方法。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable success in a wide range
of tasks. However, their reasoning capabilities, particularly in complex
domains like mathematics, remain a significant challenge. Value-based process
verifiers, which estimate the probability of a partial reasoning chain leading
to a correct solution, are a promising approach for improving reasoning.
Nevertheless, their effectiveness is often hindered by estimation error in
their training annotations, a consequence of the limited number of Monte Carlo
(MC) samples feasible due to the high cost of LLM inference. In this paper, we
identify that the estimation error primarily arises from high variance rather
than bias, and the MC estimator is a Minimum Variance Unbiased Estimator
(MVUE). To address the problem, we propose the \textsc{Com}pound \textsc{M}onte
\textsc{C}arlo \textsc{S}ampling (ComMCS) method, which constructs an unbiased
estimator by linearly combining the MC estimators from the current and
subsequent steps. Theoretically, we show that our method leads to a predictable
reduction in variance, while maintaining an unbiased estimation without
additional LLM inference cost. We also perform empirical experiments on the
MATH-500 and GSM8K benchmarks to demonstrate the effectiveness of our method.
Notably, ComMCS outperforms regression-based optimization method by 2.8 points,
the non-variance-reduced baseline by 2.2 points on MATH-500 on Best-of-32
sampling experiment.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MSRS框架通过子空间表示微调来实现多属性的联合引导。它为每个属性分配正交子空间以减少干扰，并采用混合子空间组合策略（包含特定属性子空间和共享子空间），通过动态权重函数进行整合。在推理时，MSRS引入了token级引导机制，动态识别并干预语义上最相关的token。

Result: MSRS显著减少了属性冲突，在多种属性上超越了现有方法，并能有效地泛化到不同的下游任务。

Conclusion: MSRS通过分配正交子空间来减少属性间的干扰，并结合了特定属性子空间和共享子空间，通过动态权重函数实现精确控制。实验结果表明，MSRS显著减少了属性冲突，在多种属性上优于现有方法，并能有效地泛化到不同的下游任务。

Abstract: Activation steering offers a promising approach to controlling the behavior
of Large Language Models by directly manipulating their internal activations.
However, most existing methods struggle to jointly steer multiple attributes,
often resulting in interference and undesirable trade-offs. To address this
challenge, we propose Multi-Subspace Representation Steering (MSRS), a novel
framework for effective multi-attribute steering via subspace representation
fine-tuning. MSRS reduces inter-attribute interference by allocating orthogonal
subspaces to each attribute, isolating their influence within the model's
representation space. MSRS also incorporates a hybrid subspace composition
strategy: it combines attribute-specific subspaces for unique steering
directions with a shared subspace for common steering directions. A dynamic
weighting function learns to efficiently integrate these components for precise
control. During inference, MSRS introduces a token-level steering mechanism
that dynamically identifies and intervenes on the most semantically relevant
tokens, enabling fine-grained behavioral modulation. Experimental results show
that MSRS significantly reduces attribute conflicts, surpasses existing methods
across a range of attributes, and generalizes effectively to diverse downstream
tasks.

### [222] [STEP: Stepwise Curriculum Learning for Context-Knowledge Fusion in Conversational Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10669)

Motivation: Existing conversational recommender systems (CRSs) struggle to capture deep semantics of user preferences and dialogue context, especially in integrating external knowledge graph (KG) information into dialogue generation and recommendation. Traditional approaches often fail to handle complex semantic relationships, leading to recommendations that may not align with user expectations.

Method: STEP, a conversational recommender centered on pre-trained language models, combines curriculum-guided context-knowledge fusion with lightweight task-specific prompt tuning. It uses an F-Former to progressively align dialogue context with knowledge graph entities through a three-stage curriculum, resolving fine-grained semantic mismatches. Result: STEP resolves fine-grained semantic mismatches and allows for sharing cross-task semantics while respecting distinct objectives of dialogue and recommendation.

Abstract: Conversational recommender systems (CRSs) aim to proactively capture user
preferences through natural language dialogue and recommend high-quality items.

approaches typically combine KG information directly with dialogue content,
which often struggles with complex semantic relationships, resulting in
recommendations that may not align with user expectations.
  To address these challenges, we introduce STEP, a conversational recommender
centered on pre-trained language models that combines curriculum-guided
context-knowledge fusion with lightweight task-specific prompt tuning. At its
heart, an F-Former progressively aligns the dialogue context with
knowledge-graph entities through a three-stage curriculum, thus resolving
fine-grained semantic mismatches. The fused representation is then injected
into the frozen language model via two minimal yet adaptive prefix prompts: a
conversation prefix that steers response generation toward user intent and a
recommendation prefix that biases item ranking toward knowledge-consistent
candidates. This dual-prompt scheme allows the model to share cross-task
semantics while respecting the distinct objectives of dialogue and
recommendation. Experimental results show that STEP outperforms mainstream
methods in the precision of recommendation and dialogue quality in two public
datasets.

</details>


### [223] [Scaling Up without Fading Out: Goal-Aware Sparse GNN for RL-based Generalized Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10747)
*Sangwoo Jeon,Juchul Shin,Gyeong-Tae Kim,YeonJe Cho,Seongwoo Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 通过使用稀疏、目标感知的图神经网络来改进深度强化学习中的规划，以解决大规模规划问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将规划状态表示为全连接图，导致边信息呈组合式爆炸增长，并且随着问题规模的增长，特别是网格状环境，会出现显着的稀疏性，节点信息稀释，内存需求呈指数级增长，最终导致学习在更大规模的问题上不可行。

Method: 提出了一种稀疏、目标感知图神经网络表示，该表示选择性地编码了相关的局部关系，并明确地整合了与目标相关的空间特征。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够有效地扩展到先前具有密集图表示的网格尺寸，并显著提高了策略泛化和成功率。

Conclusion: 该方法为解决大规模泛化规划任务奠定了实际基础。

Abstract: Generalized planning using deep reinforcement learning (RL) combined with
graph neural networks (GNNs) has shown promising results in various symbolic
planning domains described by PDDL. However, existing approaches typically
represent planning states as fully connected graphs, leading to a combinatorial
explosion in edge information and substantial sparsity as problem scales grow,
especially evident in large grid-based environments. This dense representation
results in diluted node-level information, exponentially increases memory
requirements, and ultimately makes learning infeasible for larger-scale
problems. To address these challenges, we propose a sparse, goal-aware GNN
representation that selectively encodes relevant local relationships and
explicitly integrates spatial features related to the goal. We validate our
approach by designing novel drone mission scenarios based on PDDL within a grid
world, effectively simulating realistic mission execution environments. Our
experimental results demonstrate that our method scales effectively to larger
grid sizes previously infeasible with dense graph representations and
substantially improves policy generalization and success rates. Our findings
provide a practical foundation for addressing realistic, large-scale
generalized planning tasks.

### [225] [Modeling Human Responses to Multimodal AI Content](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10769)
*Zhiqi Shen,Shaojing Fan,Danni Xu,Terence Sim,Mohan Kankanhalli*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过MhAIM数据集分析了人们对AI生成内容的反应，发现结合文本和视觉效果能提高识别率。研究提出了衡量用户判断和参与度的新指标，并开发了T-Lens系统，旨在使LLM具备人类意识，以应对AI驱动的错误信息风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能生成内容的普及，错误信息的风险也在增加。虽然 prior research 主要集中在识别内容是否真实，但对于此类内容如何影响人类的感知和行为知之甚少。在交易或股票市场等领域，预测人们的反应（例如，新闻帖子是否会疯传）可能比验证其事实准确性更重要。

Method: 我们引入了MhAIM数据集，该数据集包含154,552个在线帖子（其中111,153个是人工智能生成的），能够对人们如何响应人工智能生成的内容进行大规模分析。我们的人类研究表明，当帖子同时包含文本和视觉效果时，人们能更好地识别人工智能内容，特别是当两者之间存在不一致时。我们提出了三个新指标：可信度、影响力、开放性，用于量化用户如何判断和参与在线内容。我们提出了T-Lens，一个基于大型语言模型的代理系统，通过整合预测的对多模态信息的人类响应来回答用户查询。其核心是HR-MCP（人类响应模型上下文协议），它基于标准化的模型上下文协议（MCP），能够与任何大型语言模型无缝集成。

Result: 我们的人类研究表明，当帖子同时包含文本和视觉效果时，人们能更好地识别人工智能内容，特别是当两者之间存在不一致时。我们提出了三个新指标：可信度、影响力、开放性，用于量化用户如何判断和参与在线内容。我们提出的T-Lens系统通过整合预测的对多模态信息的人类响应来回答用户查询，从而更好地与人类反应保持一致，增强了可解释性和交互能力。

Conclusion: 我们的工作提供了实证见解和实用工具，使大型语言模型具备人类意识能力。通过强调人工智能、人类认知和信息接收之间的复杂相互作用，我们的研究结果为减轻人工智能驱动的错误信息的风险提供了可行的策略。

Abstract: As AI-generated content becomes widespread, so does the risk of
misinformation. While prior research has primarily focused on identifying
whether content is authentic, much less is known about how such content
influences human perception and behavior. In domains like trading or the stock
market, predicting how people react (e.g., whether a news post will go viral),
can be more critical than verifying its factual accuracy. To address this, we
take a human-centered approach and introduce the MhAIM Dataset, which contains
154,552 online posts (111,153 of them AI-generated), enabling large-scale
analysis of how people respond to AI-generated content. Our human study reveals
that people are better at identifying AI content when posts include both text
and visuals, particularly when inconsistencies exist between the two. We
propose three new metrics: trustworthiness, impact, and openness, to quantify
how users judge and engage with online content. We present T-Lens, an LLM-based
agent system designed to answer user queries by incorporating predicted human
responses to multimodal information. At its core is HR-MCP (Human Response
Model Context Protocol), built on the standardized Model Context Protocol
(MCP), enabling seamless integration with any LLM. This integration allows
T-Lens to better align with human reactions, enhancing both interpretability
and interaction capabilities. Our work provides empirical insights and
practical tools to equip LLMs with human-awareness capabilities. By
highlighting the complex interplay among AI, human cognition, and information
reception, our findings suggest actionable strategies for mitigating the risks
of AI-driven misinformation.

### [226] [The Knowledge-Reasoning Dissociation: Fundamental Limitations of LLMs in Clinical Natural Language Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10777)
*Maël Jullien,Marco Valentino,André Freitas*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLM在医学推理方面表现不佳，尽管它们拥有相关知识，但缺乏结构化的内部表征来可靠地运用知识。 GKMRV方法可以区分知识和推理，并用于评估LLM的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大规模语言模型（LLM）通过扩展数据和参数是否能获得日益结构化、可泛化的内部表征的假设。

Method: 通过引入一个包含因果归因、组合基础、认知验证和风险状态抽象四种推理类型的临床试验自然语言推理基准，并为每个条目设计了目标性的地面知识和元推理验证（GKMRV）探针，以区分事实获取失败和推理失败。评估了六种当代LLM在直接提示和思维链提示下的表现。

Result: 在GKMRV准确率方面，模型表现接近完美（平均准确率0.918），但在主要的推理任务上表现不佳（平均准确率0.25）。尽管准确率低，但输出推断在不同样本间高度一致（平均0.87），表明模型系统性地应用了潜在的启发式方法和捷径。

Conclusion: 目前的LLM在医学知识获取方面表现良好，但其内部表征的结构化和可组合性存在根本性的局限，导致它们无法可靠地运用这些知识。 GKMRV方法能够明确区分知识获取与推理能力，为评估高风险领域LLM的可靠性提供了一个有效的框架。

Abstract: Large language models are often assumed to acquire increasingly structured,
generalizable internal representations simply by scaling data and parameters.
We interrogate this assumption by introducing a Clinical Trial Natural Language
Inference benchmark comprising four reasoning families, Causal Attribution,
Compositional Grounding, Epistemic Verification, and Risk State Abstraction.
Each item is paired with a targeted Ground Knowledge and Meta-Level Reasoning
Verification (GKMRV) probe, allowing us to dissociate failures of factual
access from failures of inference. We evaluate six contemporary LLMs under both
direct and chain of thought prompting.
  Models achieve near-ceiling GKMRV accuracy (mean accuracy 0.918) yet perform
poorly on the main reasoning tasks (mean accuracy 0.25). Despite low accuracy,
output inferences are highly consistent across samples (mean 0.87), indicating
a systematic application of underlying heuristics and shortcuts.
  These results reveal fundamental structural and representational limitations:
current LLMs often possess the relevant clinical knowledge but lack the
structured, composable internal representations needed to deploy it reliably
(e.g., integrating constraints, weighing evidence, or simulating
counterfactuals). Decoupling knowledge from reasoning with GKMRV makes this
dissociation explicit and measurable, providing an effective framework for
probing the reliability of LLMs in high-stakes domains.

</details>


### [227] [Who Benefits from AI Explanations? Towards Accessible and Interpretable Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10806)
*Maria J. P. Peixoto,Akriti Pandey,Ahsan Zaman,Peter R. Lewis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究调查了 XAI 的可访问性，重点关注视障用户。研究发现，大多数 XAI 方法都依赖视觉格式，并且很少包括残疾用户。为了提高包容性，研究人员提出了一个包括 AI 系统分类、用户画像、原型设计和评估的方法。初步结果表明，简化的解释和多模式呈现对非视觉用户更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过文献综述（79 项研究）和四部分方法论概念验证来解决 XAI 的可访问性差距，该概念验证侧重于包容性 XAI 设计。

Result: 文献综述显示 XAI 技术很少包括残疾用户，并且大多数解释都依赖于视觉格式。概念验证表明，简化的非视觉解释和多模式呈现可提高可解释性。

Conclusion: 大多数 XAI 技术评估很少包括残疾用户，并且大多数解释都依赖于本质上是视觉的格式。初步研究表明，对于非视觉用户而言，简化的解释比详细的解释更易于理解，并且需要多模式呈现才能实现更公平的可解释性。

Abstract: As AI systems are increasingly deployed to support decision-making in
critical domains, explainability has become a means to enhance the
understandability of these outputs and enable users to make more informed and
conscious choices. However, despite growing interest in the usability of
eXplainable AI (XAI), the accessibility of these methods, particularly for
users with vision impairments, remains underexplored. This paper investigates
accessibility gaps in XAI through a two-pronged approach. First, a literature
review of 79 studies reveals that evaluations of XAI techniques rarely include
disabled users, with most explanations relying on inherently visual formats.
Second, we present a four-part methodological proof of concept that
operationalizes inclusive XAI design: (1) categorization of AI systems, (2)
persona definition and contextualization, (3) prototype design and
implementation, and (4) expert and user assessment of XAI techniques for
accessibility. Preliminary findings suggest that simplified explanations are
more comprehensible for non-visual users than detailed ones, and that
multimodal presentation is required for more equitable interpretability.

### [228] [Universal intrinsic orbital dynamics from Berry curvature in electronic two-band systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10385)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The geometric structure of quantum states plays a fundamental role in
determining the intrinsic dynamics of electrons in solids. In this work, we
study the geometric origin of orbital angular momentum and its transport in a
general two-band electronic system. Without assuming any symmetry or
dimensional constraints, we show that the orbital Berry curvature, which
governs the orbital Hall effect, can be universally expressed as the product of
the band energy and the square of the Berry curvature. This highlights the
central role of Berry curvature in engineering orbital Hall responses. We also
discuss the applicability of our framework by analyzing a realistic model. Our
findings underscore the geometric universality of itinerant intrinsic orbital
dynamics.

### [229] [Edgetronics in 2D Altermagnet via Real-Space-Spin Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10451)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索实空间-自旋（r-s）耦合在二维交变磁性二阶拓扑绝缘体中的应用，以期在自旋电子学领域实现高效的自旋操控。

Method: 本研究通过计算设计了一种基于Cr2Se2O单层的边缘隧道磁电阻（edge-TMR）器件，以验证其边缘传输和通过尼尔序或电场进行控制的可能性。

Result: 研究发现，一维r-s耦合在二维交变磁性二阶拓扑绝缘体中表现出一种新的浮栅态，该浮栅态具有尼尔矢量依赖性和电可调控性，并能产生一种可开关的边缘隧道磁电阻（edge-TMR）效应。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了一维实空间-自旋（r-s）耦合在一维d-超导的二阶拓扑绝缘体中的意外表现，其中出现了一类不依赖于动量-自旋（k-s）耦合的浮栅态。这些浮栅态具有由尼尔矢量决定的、可电调控的特性，为自旋电子学提供了一种新的实现自旋操控的途径。

Abstract: The coupling between real-space coordinates and spin (r-s) provides an
alternative route to achieve efficient spin manipulation in spintronics beyond
the conventional momentum-spin (k-s) coupling paradigm. Here we demonstrate an
unexpected manifestation of one-dimensional (1D) r-s coupling in
two-dimensional (2D) altermagnetic second-order topological insulators, where
the spin-split floating edge states - energetically isolated within the bulk
band gap - emerge and exhibit both Neel-vector-dependent and electrically
tunable behaviors. The 1D edge-spin r-s coupling ensures carrier transport to
be exclusively carried by the edge states with quantized spin conductance,
giving rise to an unconventional edge tunnel magnetoresistance (edge-TMR)
effect that can be switched On or Off. As a proof of concept, we
computationally design an edge-TMR device based on Cr2Se2O monolayer to
demonstrate its edge transportation and controllability via the Neel order or
electric field. Our findings propose a general prototype altermagnetic device
for next-generation low-dimensional spintronics.

### [230] [Periodic transitions of topological charge in skyrmions confined within FeGe and Co/Pt nanodisks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10607)
*R. L. Silva,R. C. Silva*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 研究了FeGe和Co/Pt中通过磁场诱导斯格明子拓扑电荷的周期性反转，揭示了不同的动态机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在自旋电子学应用中实现斯格明子，动态控制其极性、涡度和拓扑电荷至关重要。

Method: 通过施加垂直于薄膜平面的振荡磁场，在FeGe（一种块状手性磁体）和Co/Pt（具有强Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用的界面体系）中诱导自旋纹理的循环转变，研究拓扑电荷的周期性反转。

Result: 在FeGe中，斯格明子通过中间斯格明子物态经历了 $Q=1 ightarrow 0 ightarrow -1$ 的演化；在Co/Pt中，该过程涉及斯格明子的湮灭和重形核，导致拓扑电荷交替变化。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了在FeGe和Co/Pt两种体系中，通过周期性地改变拓扑电荷来动态调控斯格明子性质的两种不同机制，为基于斯格明子的器件的节能控制提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: The dynamic control of skyrmion properties such as polarity, vorticity, and
topological charge is crucial for their implementation in spintronic
applications. In this work, we investigate the periodic inversion of the
topological charge in two distinct systems: FeGe, a bulk chiral magnet, and
Co/Pt, an interfacial system with strong Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction. By
applying an oscillating magnetic field perpendicular to the film plane, we
induce cyclic transitions in the spin texture. In FeGe, the skyrmion evolves
through a $Q=1 \rightarrow 0 \rightarrow -1$ sequence via an intermediate
skyrmionium state. In Co/Pt, the process involves skyrmion annihilation and
re-nucleation, resulting in alternating topological charges. These results
reveal distinct dynamic mechanisms for topological charge modulation, offering
potential pathways for the energy-efficient control of skyrmion-based devices.

### [231] [Edge Reconstruction in a Quantum Spin Hall Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10726)
*Rahul Soni,Matthias Thamm,Gonzalo Alvarez,Bernd Rosenow,Adrian Del Maestro*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 相互作用导致量子自旋霍尔绝缘体边缘出现轨道选择性自旋极化，可能破坏拓扑保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究相互作用驱动下量子自旋霍尔绝缘体的边缘重建现象。

Method: 采用实空间密度矩阵重整化群方法（R DMRG），在总系综和正则系综下，研究了由Kanamori-Hubbard相互作用描述的Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang模型。

Result: 在二维圆柱体中，发现了导致自旋极化边缘态的离散粒子数跃迁，该态由新兴的铁磁交换相互作用稳定。重建是轨道选择性的，主要发生在s轨道通道。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了一种量子自旋霍尔绝缘体边缘重建的微观机制，该机制可能危及由时间反转对称性提供的拓扑保护。

Abstract: We study interaction-driven edge reconstruction in a quantum spin Hall
insulator described by the Bernevig-Hughes-Zhang model with Kanamori-Hubbard
interactions using the real-space density matrix renormalization group method
in both the grand-canonical and canonical ensembles. For a two-dimensional
cylinder with a smooth edge, we identify discrete particle-number transitions
that lead to a spin-polarized edge state stabilized by an emergent
ferromagnetic exchange interaction. The reconstruction is orbital-selective,
occurring predominantly in the $s$-orbital channel. Our results reveal a fully
microscopic mechanism for emergent spin polarization at the edge that could
compromise the topological protection of helical edge states by time reversal
symmetry.

</details>


### [232] [Reinforcement-Learning-Designed Field-Free Sub-Nanosecond Spin-Orbit-Torque Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10792)
*Yuta Igarashi,Junji Fujimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 强化学习在300皮秒内实现了纳米磁体的磁化反转，并揭示了其中的物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在电流密度下，通过强化学习自动发现电流波形，最小化磁化轨迹路径，并利用进动捷径，在更短的时间内实现磁化反转。

Method: 通过将强化学习（RL）与基于自旋-轨道力矩（SOT）的朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特方程耦合，实现了对单畴纳米磁体的磁化反转。

Result: 成功在300皮秒内实现了确定性的、无外加磁场条件下，单畴纳米磁体的磁化反转，并通过学习到的脉冲提取了清晰的物理动力学图像，建立了反转时间的理论下界，并讨论了实验实现的可能性。

Conclusion: 该研究实现了300皮秒内确定性的、无外加磁场条件下，通过强化学习（RL）与基于自旋-轨道力矩（SOT）的朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特方程的耦合，对单畴纳米磁体的磁化反转。RL代理自动发现电流波形，最小化磁化轨迹路径，并利用了场力矩和硬轴磁异向性实现的进动捷径。

Abstract: We demonstrate deterministic, field-free magnetization reversal of a
single-domain nanomagnet within 300 ps under a current density of $3 \times
10^{10}~\mathrm{A/m^2}$ by coupling reinforcement learning (RL) to the
Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation with the spin-orbit torques (SOTs). The RL
agent autonomously discovers a current waveform that minimizes the
magnetization trajectory path and exploits a precessional shortcut enabled by
the field-like SOT and hard-axis anisotropy. From the learned pulse, we extract
a clear physical picture of the dynamics and develop a model-based analytical
framework that establishes a lower bound on the switching time. The control
strategy remains robust across a wide range of damping constants and is
stabilized against thermal fluctuations at higher current densities. We also
discuss feasible experimental implementations for the precessional switching.

### [233] [Dynamically tunable hydrodynamic transport in boron nitride-encapsulated graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10846)
*Akash Gugnani,Aniket Majumdar,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Arindam Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过紫外线和栅极电场调控石墨烯器件的无序水平，实现了对电荷流体动力学的动态控制，并观察到器件趋向于恢复维德曼-弗朗茨（WF）定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管石墨烯因其高质量器件的可用性而成为研究电子流粘滞性的有希望的候选材料，但传统的器件制备过程限制了在同一器件中实现从以杂质为主的输运到粘滞输运的调控。本研究旨在克服这一限制，探索一种在同一器件中动态调控电荷流动机制的方法。

Method: 本研究利用紫外线（UV）辐射和栅极电场相结合的方法，对单层石墨烯器件中的电荷流体动力学进行了动态调控。通过改变紫外线照射强度来调节石墨烯的无序水平，并在此过程中监测其热电输运性质，特别是与维德曼-弗朗茨（WF）定律的偏离程度，以量化电荷流体动力学的变化。

Result: 本研究成功地实现了在室温下通过紫外线辐射和栅极电场动态调控单层石墨烯器件中的电荷流体动力学。研究观察到，随着紫外线辐射的增加，动量弛豫散射相对于电子间散射急剧增加，洛伦兹数也增加了近十倍，表现出器件的无序水平在提高，并趋向于恢复维德曼-弗朗茨（WF）定律。

Conclusion: 本研究通过结合紫外线（UV）辐射和栅极电场，首次实现了在同一石墨烯器件中动态调控电荷流体动力学的能力，并在室温下通过单层石墨烯器件的宏观热电输运性质，特别是与维德曼-弗朗茨（WF）定律的偏离程度来量化这种调控。通过使用紫外线照射在封装的六方氮化硼（hBN）电介质中产生瞬时陷阱态，我们实现了对无序水平的连续可逆调控。随着紫外线辐射的增加，动量弛豫散射相对于电子间散射急剧增加，洛伦兹数也增加了近十倍，使得高度无序的石墨烯趋向于恢复WF定律。我们的实验为调控先进石墨烯器件中电荷流动的基本机制提供了一种有效策略。

Abstract: Over the past decade, graphene has emerged as a promising candidate for
exploring the viscous nature of electronic flow facilitated by the availability
of extremely high-quality devices employing a graphene channel encapsulated
within dielectric layers of hexagonal boron nitride (hBN). However, the level
of disorder in such systems is mainly determined by the device fabrication
protocols, making it impossible to obtain a tunability between the
impurity-dominated and the viscous transport within the same device. In this
work, using a combination of ultraviolet (UV) radiation and gate electric
field, we have demonstrated a dynamic modulation of charge hydrodynamics,
quantified in the thermal and electrical transport by the extent of departure
from the Wiedemann-Franz (WF) Law in monolayer graphene devices at room
temperature. We achieved this by tuning the disorder level continuously and
reversibly using UV light to create transient trap states in the encapsulating
hBN dielectric. With progressive UV radiation, we observed a dramatic increase
in the momentum-relaxing scattering relative to that between the electrons and
also the Lorentz number, by nearly a factor of ten, with increasing disorder,
thereby approaching the restoration of the WF law in highly disordered
graphene. Our experiments outline a potent strategy to tune the fundamental
mechanism of charge flow in state-of-the-art graphene devices.

</details>


### [234] [Interaction enhanced inter-site hoppings for holons and interlayer exciton insulators in moiré correlated insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10847)
*Zijian Ma,Hongyi Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: Correlated insulators in moir'e-patterned TMDs show enhanced hopping for holons and interlayer excitons due to Coulomb interactions, with calculated Bohr radius and energy splitting for the latter.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To theoretically investigate the nearest-neighbor inter-site hoppings of holons and interlayer exciton insulators in moir'e-patterned van der Waals structures of transition metal dichalcogenides.

Method: Theoretical investigation of nearest-neighbor inter-site hoppings of holons and interlayer exciton insulators.

Result: Hopping strengths are significantly enhanced compared to a single carrier. The effective Bohr radius and energy splitting between the ground and first-excited states for the interlayer exciton insulator have been obtained.

Conclusion: The hopping strengths of holons and interlayer exciton insulators are significantly enhanced due to strong Coulomb interaction between carriers at different sites. The effective Bohr radius and energy splitting for the interlayer exciton insulator have also been obtained.

Abstract: In moir\'e-patterned van der Waals structures of transition metal
dichalcogenides, correlated insulators can form under integer and fractional
fillings, whose transport properties are governed by various quasiparticle
excitations including holons, doublons and interlayer exciton insulators. Here
we theoretically investigate the nearest-neighbor inter-site hoppings of holons
and interlayer exciton insulators. Our analysis indicates that these hopping
strengths are significantly enhanced compared to that of a single carrier. The
underlying mechanism can be attributed to the strong Coulomb interaction
between carriers at different sites. For the interlayer exciton insulator
consisting of a holon and a carrier in different layers, we have also obtained
its effective Bohr radius and energy splitting between the ground and
first-excited states.

### [235] [Exceptional flat bands in bipartite non-Hermitian quantum crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10901)
*Juan Pablo Esparza,Vladimir Juricic*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 当一个亚晶格具有动量无关的特征值，并且其简并度超过另一个亚晶格时，无论增益、损耗或复数耦合如何，都会形成平带。在奇异点处，色散带合并形成“奇异平带”，即使在这些奇点之外也能持续存在，并表现出跨越两个亚晶格的生息模式，其能量和寿命可通过亚晶格不对称和非互易耦合进行调整。该框架统一了厄米和非厄米平带结构，并揭示了没有闭轨系统类似物的无色散态。所提出的结构适用于合成平台，从可以 त्या地模拟平带的经典超材料，到像光子晶体和超冷原子阵列这样的量子工程系统，它们应该能够承载源于这种非凡平带的关联和拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在厄米格中，平带的形成机制已经广为人知，但它们是否会持续存在，以及在与开放和驱动系统相关的非厄米（NH）量子晶体中获得新的特征，仍然是一个悬而未决的问题。

Method: 在二分格中，基于亚晶格简并失配的厄米原理可以直接扩展到非厄米（NH）区域：只要一个亚晶格在动量上具有独立的特征值，并且其简并度超过另一个亚晶格上的简并度，那么无论增益、损耗或复数耦合如何，都会产生平带。

Result: 在奇异点处，色散带合并形成“奇异平带”，即使在这些奇点之外也能持续存在，并表现出跨越两个亚晶格的生息模式，其能量和寿命可通过亚晶格不对称和非互易耦合进行调整。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了厄米和非厄米平带结构，并揭示了没有闭轨系统类似物的无色散态。所提出的结构适用于合成平台，从可以 त्या地模拟平带的经典超材料，到像光子晶体和超冷原子阵列这样的量子工程系统，它们应该能够承载源于这种非凡平带的关联和拓扑相。

Abstract: Flat bands, in which kinetic energy is quenched and quantum states become
macroscopically degenerate, host a rich variety of correlated and topological
phases, from unconventional superconductors to fractional Chern insulators. In
Hermitian lattices, their formation mechanisms are now well understood, but
whether such states persist, and acquire new features in non-Hermitian (NH)
quantum crystals, relevant to open and driven systems, has remained an open
question. Here we show that the Hermitian principle for flat-band formation in
bipartite lattices, based on a sublattice degeneracy mismatch, extends directly
to the NH regime: whenever one sublattice hosts a momentum-independent
eigenvalue with degeneracy exceeding that of its partner on the other
sublattice, flat bands arise regardless of gain, loss, or complex couplings.
Strikingly, at exceptional points, dispersive bands coalesce to form
\emph{exceptional flat bands} that persist beyond these singularities,
exhibiting biorthogonal eigenmodes spanning both sublattices, with energies and
lifetimes tunable via sublattice asymmetry and non-reciprocal couplings. This
general framework unifies Hermitian and NH flat-band constructions, and reveals
dispersionless states with no closed-system analogue. The proposed construction
is applicable to synthetic platforms, from classical metamaterials, where flat
bands can be directly emulated, to quantum-engineered systems such as photonic
crystals and ultracold atom arrays, which should host correlated and
topological phases emerging from such exceptional flat bands.

</details>

### [236] [Data-Driven Topological Analysis of Polymorphic Crystal Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10270)
*Sourin Dey,Nicholas Miklaucic,Sadman Sadeed Omee,Rongzhi Dong,Lai Wei,Qinyang Li,Nihang Fu,Jianjun Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究利用数据分析和拓扑嵌入技术，发现拓扑结构是影响材料多晶性的关键因素，有助于加速多晶材料的发现与设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多晶现象在决定材料的物理、化学和功能特性方面起着至关重要的作用，准确识别和预测多晶结构对于材料设计、药物开发和器件优化至关重要，因为未知或被忽视的多晶型可能导致意外的性能或稳定性问题。然而，由于分子构象、晶体堆积和对称性约束之间复杂的相互作用，直接从化学成分预测多晶性仍然是一个挑战。

Method: 利用 Materials Project 数据库进行全面的数据驱动分析，研究多晶材料的成分、空间群分布和多面体结构单元，构建多面体连接图并嵌入其拓扑结构，以实现对多晶材料的聚类和相似性分析。

Result: 研究发现了频繁出现于不同空间群的多晶对（例如 (71, 225)）具有持续存在的共同拓扑模式，揭示了许多多晶在对称性和堆积不同但局部多面体环境保持一致，通过拓扑嵌入成功地将不同空间群中的多晶及结构相似材料进行聚类，证明了拓扑相似性在多晶行为描述中的潜力。

Conclusion: 该研究通过数据驱动分析揭示了多晶材料的结构特征，强调了拓扑结构而非对称性是多晶重复的关键因素，并展示了拓扑相似性作为描述多晶行为的有力工具，为加速多晶发现和设计提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Polymorphism, the ability of a compound to crystallize in multiple distinct
structures, plays a vital role in determining the physical, chemical, and
functional properties of materials. Accurate identification and prediction of
polymorphic structures are critical for materials design, drug development, and
device optimization, as unknown or overlooked polymorphs may lead to unexpected
performance or stability issues. Despite its significance, predicting
polymorphism directly from a chemical composition remains a challenging problem
due to the complex interplay between molecular conformations, crystal packing,
and symmetry constraints. In this study, we conduct a comprehensive data-driven
analysis of polymorphic materials from the Materials Project database,
uncovering key statistical patterns in their composition, space group
distributions, and polyhedral building blocks. We discover that frequent
polymorph pairs across space groups, such as (71, 225), display recurring
topological motifs that persist across different compounds, highlighting
topology not symmetry alone as a key factor in polymorphic recurrence. We
reveal that many polymorphs exhibit consistent local polyhedral environments
despite differences in their symmetry or packing. Additionally, by constructing
polyhedron connectivity graphs and embedding their topology, we successfully
cluster polymorphs and structurally similar materials even across different
space groups, demonstrating that topological similarity serves as a powerful
descriptor for polymorphic behavior. Our findings provide new insights into the
structural characteristics of polymorphic materials and demonstrate the
potential of data mining and machine learning for accelerating polymorph
discovery and design.

</details>


### [237] [Atomistic Description of Spin Crossover Under Pressure and its Giant Barocaloric Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10334)
*S. Vela,J. Ribas-Ariño,S. P. Vallone,A. M. dos Santos,M. A. Halcrow,K. G. Sandeman*

Abstract: The pressure-dependent evolution of the spin crossover (SCO) transition has
garnered significant interest due to its connection to the giant barocaloric
effect (BCE) near room temperature. Pressure alters both the molecular and
solid-state structures of SCO materials, affecting the relative stability of
low- and high-spin states and, consequently, the transition temperature

influences its SCO transition, including the onset of a phase transition, as
well as the key role of low-frequency phonons in the BCE. Furthermore, we
establish a computational protocol for accurately modeling the BCE in SCO
crystals, providing a powerful tool for the rapid and efficient discovery of
new materials with enhanced barocaloric performance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一个名为 EDIS（电极动态离子嵌入/脱出模拟器）的软件平台，该平台利用高精度的机器学习势能，能够模拟电极材料中动态的离子嵌入和脱出过程，并能实现接近量子力学方法的精度。

Result: EDIS 能够高效地模拟不同充放电状态下的结构演变和锂离子扩散行为，并支持对锂离子浓度和分布变化如何影响锂离子输运性质进行定量分析，评估结构缺陷的影响，以及跟踪连续循环过程中的结构演变和输运特性。

Abstract: As the core determinant of lithium-ion battery performance, electrode

stability, and durability. During charging and discharging, electrode materials
undergo complex ion intercalation and deintercalation processes, accompanied by
defect formation and structural evolution. However, the microscopic mechanisms
underlying processes such as cation disordering, lattice oxygen loss, and stage
structure formation phenomena are still not fully understood. To address these
challenges, we have developed the Electrode Dynamic Ion
Intercalation/Deintercalation Simulator (EDIS), a software platform designed to
simulate the dynamic processes of ion intercalation and deintercalation in
electrode materials. Leveraging high-precision machine learning potentials,
EDIS can efficiently model structural evolution and lithium-ion diffusion
behavior under various states of charge and discharge, achieving accuracy
approaching that of quantum mechanical methods in relevant chemical spaces. The
software supports quantitative analysis of how variations in lithium-ion
concentration and distribution affect lithium-ion transport properties, enables
evaluation of the impact of structural defects, and allows for tracking of both
structural evolution and transport characteristics during continuous cycling.
EDIS is versatile and can be extended to sodium-ion batteries and related
systems. By enabling in-depth analysis of these microscopic processes, EDIS
provides a robust theoretical tool for mechanistic studies and the rational
design of high-performance electrode materials for next-generation lithium-ion
batteries.

### [240] [FastTrack: a fast method to evaluate mass transport in solid leveraging universal machine learning interatomic potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10505)
*Hanwen Kang,Tenglong Lu,Zhanbin Qi,Jiandong Guo,Sheng Meng,Miao Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于机器学习力场（MLFF）和三维势能面（PES）采样与插值的新框架，用于快速准确地计算晶体原子迁移势垒，速度相比DFT-NEB提升约100倍，准确性与DFT和实验相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介绍了一种用于计算晶体中原子迁移势垒的快速、准确的框架。

Method: 通过结合通用机器学习力场（MLFF）、三维势能面（PES）采样和插值来计算晶体中原子的迁移势垒。该方法通过超胞扩展抑制周期性自相互作用，在空间网格上从MLFF能量构建连续PES，并提取最小能量路径，无需预定义NEB图像。

Result: 在十二种锂离子电池电极和电解质材料（包括LiCoO2、LiFePO4和LGPS）上的测试结果表明，该方法计算出的势垒与DFT和实验结果的偏差在几十 meV 以内，并且速度比DFT-NEB快约100倍。此外，该研究还评估了GPTFF、CHGNet和MACE等模型，并证明了使用PBE/PBE+U数据进行微调可以进一步提高准确性。

Conclusion: 所提出的机器学习力场（MLFF）结合三维势能面采样和插值的方法，能够快速准确地计算晶体中原子的迁移势垒，并且在准确性上接近第一性原理计算（DFT）和实验结果，同时速度提升约100倍。

Abstract: We introduce a rapid, accurate framework for computing atomic migration
barriers in crystals by combining universal machine learning force fields
(MLFFs) with 3D potential energy surface sampling and interpolation. Our method
suppresses periodic self interactions via supercell expansion, builds a
continuous PES from MLFF energies on a spatial grid, and extracts minimum
energy pathways without predefined NEB images. Across twelve benchmark
electrode and electrolyte materials including LiCoO2, LiFePO4, and LGPS our
MLFF-derived barriers lie within tens of meV of DFT and experiment, while
achieving ~10^2 x speedups over DFT-NEB. We benchmark GPTFF, CHGNet, and MACE,
show that fine-tuning on PBE/PBE+U data further enhances accuracy, and provide
an open-source package for high-throughput materials screening and interactive
PES visualization.

</details>

predictions are excluded by the measurement data which means that the currently

Abstract: Semiconductor materials are the foundation of modern electronics, and their
functionality is dictated by the interactions between fundamental excitations
occurring on (sub-)picosecond timescales. Using time-resolved Raman
spectroscopy and transient reflectivity measurements, we shed light on the
ultrafast dynamics in germanium. We observe an increase in the optical phonon
temperature in the first few picoseconds, driven by the energy transfer from
photoexcited holes, and the subsequent decay into acoustic phonons through
anharmonic coupling. Moreover, the temperature, Raman frequency, and linewidth
of this phonon mode show strikingly different decay dynamics. This difference
was ascribed to the local thermal strain generated by the ultrafast excitation.
We also observe Brillouin oscillations, given by a strain pulse traveling
through germanium, whose damping is correlated to the optical phonon mode.
These findings, supported by density functional theory and molecular dynamics
simulations, provide a better understanding of the energy dissipation
mechanisms in semiconductors.

Abstract: Chiral soliton lattices (CSLs) are nontrivial spin textures that emerge from

magnetic fields. While well established in monoaxial helimagnets, their role in
materials with anisotropic, direction-dependent chirality remains poorly
understood. Here, we report the direct observation of a tunable transition from
$\pi$ to 2$\pi$ soliton lattices in the non-centrosymmetric Heusler compound
Mn1.4PtSn. Using Lorentz transmission electron microscopy, resonant elastic

magnetic ground state, in contrast to the expected helical phase, which evolves
into a classical 2$\pi$-CSL under increasing out-of-plane magnetic fields. This

magnetocrystalline anisotropy and magnetostatic interactions, as captured by a
double sine-Gordon model. Our analysis not only reveals the microscopic
mechanisms stabilizing these soliton lattices but also demonstrates their
general relevance to materials with D2d, S4, Cnv, or Cn symmetries. The results
establish a broadly applicable framework for understanding magnetic phase
diagrams in chiral systems, with implications for soliton-based spintronic
devices and topological transport phenomena.

### [245] [Symmetry-Constrained Multi-Scale Physics-Informed Neural Networks for Graphene Electronic Band Structure Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10718)
*Wei Shan Lee,I Hang Kwok,Kam Ian Leong,Chi Kiu Althina Chau,Kei Chon Sio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在计算效率和物理精度之间难以平衡，而准确预测二维材料的电子能带结构仍然是一个基本挑战。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SCMS-PINN (v35) 的方法，该方法直接学习石墨烯的能带结构，并通过多头架构强制执行晶体对称性。该方法使用三个专门的 ResNet-6 通道（K-head、M-head 和 General head）处理从 k 点提取的 31 个物理信息特征。通过渐进式狄拉克约束调度，从 5.0 逐步增加到 25.0 的权重参数，实现了从全局拓扑到局部关键物理的层次化学习。所有十二个 C$_{6v}$ 运算通过系统平均强制执行。

Result: 在 10,000 个 k 点上训练 300 个 epoch 后，训练损失降低了 99.99%（从 34.597 到 0.003），验证损失为 0.0085。模型预测的狄拉克点间隙在理论零值 30.3 μeV 以内，在整个布里渊区实现了 53.9 meV（价带）和 40.5 meV（导带）的平均误差。所有十二个 C$_{6v}$ 运算均通过系统平均强制执行，保证了精确的对称性保持。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of electronic band structures in two-dimensional
materials remains a fundamental challenge, with existing methods struggling to
balance computational efficiency and physical accuracy. We present the
Symmetry-Constrained Multi-Scale Physics-Informed Neural Network (SCMS-PINN)
v35, which directly learns graphene band structures while rigorously enforcing
crystallographic symmetries through a multi-head architecture. Our approach
introduces three specialized ResNet-6 pathways -- K-head for Dirac physics,
M-head for saddle points, and General head for smooth interpolation --
operating on 31 physics-informed features extracted from k-points. Progressive
Dirac constraint scheduling systematically increases the weight parameter from
5.0 to 25.0, enabling hierarchical learning from global topology to local
critical physics. Training on 10,000 k-points over 300 epochs achieves 99.99\%
reduction in training loss (34.597 to 0.003) with validation loss of 0.0085.
The model predicts Dirac point gaps within 30.3 $\mu$eV of theoretical zero and
achieves average errors of 53.9 meV (valence) and 40.5 meV (conduction) across
the Brillouin zone. All twelve C$_{6v}$ operations are enforced through
systematic averaging, guaranteeing exact symmetry preservation. This framework
establishes a foundation for extending physics-informed learning to broader
two-dimensional materials for accelerated discovery.

substitution on the properties of quantum paraelectric SrTiO$_3$ (STO). We find

reproduce the experimentally observed isotope effect, in which replacement of
$^{16}$O by $^{18}$O induces the ferroelectric state, and demonstrate that the

displacive manner. We calculate the ferroelectric soft mode frequency as a
function of volume, lattice parameters and temperature for ST$^{16}$O and
ST$^{18}$O, and find that the phase space in which ST$^{16}$O shows quantum
paraelectric behaviour, while ST$^{18}$O becomes ferroelectric is narrow. Our
study shows that machine learning interatomic potentials enable
temperature-dependent simulations that include quantum and anharmonic phonon
effects, however quantitative prediction of phase diagrams remains challenging
due to a lack of universally accurate electronic structure methods.

### [248] [Formation and protection of an Eu-Ir surface compound below hexagonal boron nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10746)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Low energy electron diffraction (LEED), scanning tunnelling microscopy (STM), x-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS), and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) were used to examine the structural and electronic properties of Eu intercalation below hBN on an Ir(111) substrate.

Result: Different superstructures ((5 x M), (5 x 2), and (sqrt(3) x sqrt(3))R30 degrees) were identified. Eu intercalation leads to unidirectional ordering of Eu atoms, diffusion of excess Eu into the bulk in a trivalent state, and formation of a EuIr2 surface alloy with divalent Eu atoms at higher temperatures and coverage.

Conclusion: Europium (Eu) intercalation below hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) on an Ir(111) substrate results in different superstructures, including (5 x M), (5 x 2), and (sqrt(3) x sqrt(3))R30 degrees, depending on deposition temperature and coverage. Abstract: Europium (Eu) intercalation below hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) on an Ir(111)
substrate at various Eu coverages is investigated. The structural and
electronic properties were examined using low energy electron diffraction
(LEED), scanning tunnelling microscopy (STM), x-ray photoelectron spectroscopy
(XPS) and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES). Depending on the
deposition temperature, different superstructures, (5 $\times$ $M$), (5
$\times$ 2), and ($ \sqrt{3}$ $\times$ $\sqrt{3})R30^{\circ}$ with respect to
the Ir substrate were identified by LEED. The (5 $\times$ $M$) superstructure
($M$ $>$ 2), at 0.1 monolayer (ML), preserved the hBN/Ir Moir{\'e} pattern and
exhibited a unidirectional ordering of Eu atoms. At higher coverage of 0.26 ML,
a (5 $\times$ 2) superstructure emerged, where excess Eu atoms diffused into
the bulk and were analyzed as Eu in a tri-valent state. At the highest
preparation temperature with a one-third ML Eu, the formation of a ($\sqrt{3}$
$\times$ $\sqrt{3})R30^{\circ}$ superstructure indicates the presence of a
EuIr$_{2}$ surface alloy beneath the hBN layer, with di-valent Eu atoms
suggesting potential ferromagnetic properties. Air exposure was used to
evaluate the protection of the hBN layer, and the results indicate that the
EuIr$_{2}$ surface alloy was partially protected. However, the hBN layer
remained intact by intercalation and air exposure, as confirmed by ARPES
analysis.

### [249] [WiFi-based Global Localization in Large-Scale Environments Leveraging Structural Priors from osmAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.10144)
*Xu Ma,Jiajie Zhang,Fujing Xie,Sören Schwertfeger*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Error


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: Global localization is essential for autonomous robotics, especially in
indoor environments where the GPS signal is denied. We propose a novel
WiFi-based localization framework that leverages ubiquitous wireless
infrastructure and the OpenStreetMap Area Graph (osmAG) for large-scale indoor
environments. Our approach integrates signal propagation modeling with osmAG's
geometric and topological priors. In the offline phase, an iterative
optimization algorithm localizes WiFi Access Points (APs) by modeling wall
attenuation, achieving a mean localization error of 3.79 m (35.3\% improvement
over trilateration). In the online phase, real-time robot localization uses the
augmented osmAG map, yielding a mean error of 3.12 m in fingerprinted areas
(8.77\% improvement over KNN fingerprinting) and 3.83 m in non-fingerprinted
areas (81.05\% improvement). Comparison with a fingerprint-based method shows
that our approach is much more space efficient and achieves superior
localization accuracy, especially for positions where no fingerprint data are
available. Validated across a complex 11,025 &m^2& multi-floor environment,

localization, solving the kidnapped robot problem. The code and dataset are
available at https://github.com/XuMa369/osmag-wifi-localization.
